create_building_effect  = {
if = {
    limit = { NOT = { has_building = $BUILDING_TYPE$ } }
	create_building = {
		building = $BUILDING_TYPE$
		level = 1
	}
    activate_building = { building = $BUILDING_TYPE$ } 
}
else = {
    random_scope_building = {
        limit = {
            is_building_type = $BUILDING_TYPE$
        }
        state = {
            switch = {
                trigger = prev.level
1 = {create_building = {building = $BUILDING_TYPE$ level = 2}}
